# Grafana Legacy Alerting to Unified Alerting Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) engine: the legacy alert rule storage, the unified alert rule storage, and the migration script that converts legacy rules to unified format.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

package ualert

import (
	"fmt"
	"time"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/util/xorm"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator"
)

// typeKey is a vendored migration.typeKey.
var typeKey = "currentAlertingType"

// AlertingType is a vendored migration.store.AlertingType.
type alertingType string

const (
	Legacy          alertingType = "Legacy"
	UnifiedAlerting alertingType = "UnifiedAlerting"
)

// CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries creates kv store entries for each organization if the migration has been run.
// This is needed now that we've changed the semantics of data loss when upgrading / rolling back. If a user who previously
// upgraded were to rollback and upgrade again without clean_upgrade, then since they don't have org-level migrated states
// it will attempt to upgrade their orgs as if they had never upgraded before. This will almost definitely fail with
// duplicate key errors.
//
// In addition, this changes the entry for orgId=0 to be better named as it no longer tracks whether the
// migration has been run, but rather the current alerting type of Grafana; Legacy or UnifiedAlerting. This is used to
// detect transitions between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting by comparing to the desired type in the configuration.
func CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	mg.AddMigration("copy kvstore migration status to each org", &createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries{})

	// Adds back the entry for orgId=0 if it doesn't exist. This is not strictly necessary, but
	// helps to cover some issues with createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries if a grafana instance on UA is downgraded to before
	// the split for org-specific migrated statuses.
	mg.AddMigration("add back entry for orgid=0 migrated status", &addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry{})
}

     9→// Silence-specific compat functions to convert between grafana/alerting and model types.
    10→
    11→func GettableSilenceToSilence(s alertingNotify.GettableSilence) *models.Silence {
    12→	sil := models.Silence(s)
    13→	return &sil
    14→}
    15→
    16→func GettableSilencesToSilences(silences alertingNotify.GettableSilences) []*models.Silence {
    17→	res := make([]*models.Silence, 0, len(silences))
    18→	for _, sil := range silences {
    19→		res = append(res, GettableSilenceToSilence(*sil))
    20→	}
    21→	return res
    22→}
    23→
    24→func SilenceToPostableSilence(s models.Silence) *alertingNotify.PostableSilence {
    25→	var id string
    26→	if s.ID != nil {
    27→		id = *s.ID
    28→	}
    29→	return &alertingNotify.PostableSilence{
    30→		ID:      id,
    31→		Silence: s.Silence,
    32→	}
    33→}

    21→}
    22→

    27→}

    30→type InstanceStateType string
    31→
    32→const (
    33→	// InstanceStateFiring is for a firing alert.
    34→	InstanceStateFiring InstanceStateType = "Alerting"
    35→	// InstanceStateNormal is for a normal alert.
    36→	InstanceStateNormal InstanceStateType = "Normal"
    37→	// InstanceStatePending is for an alert that is firing but has not met the duration
    38→	InstanceStatePending InstanceStateType = "Pending"
    39→	// InstanceStateNoData is for an alert with no data.
    40→	InstanceStateNoData InstanceStateType = "NoData"
    41→	// InstanceStateError is for an erroring alert.
    42→	InstanceStateError InstanceStateType = "Error"
    43→	// InstanceStateRecovering is for a recovering alert.
    44→	InstanceStateRecovering InstanceStateType = "Recovering"
    45→)

    15→func (hs *HTTPServer) GetAlertNotifiers() func(*contextmodel.ReqContext) response.Response {
    16→	return func(r *contextmodel.ReqContext) response.Response {
    17→		v2 := notify.GetSchemaForAllIntegrations()
    18→		slices.SortFunc(v2, func(a, b schema.IntegrationTypeSchema) int {
    19→			return strings.Compare(string(a.Type), string(b.Type))
    20→		})
    21→		if r.Query("version") == "2" {
    22→			return response.JSON(http.StatusOK, v2)
    23→		}
    24→
    25→		type NotifierPlugin struct {
    26→			Type        string         `json:"type"`
    27→			TypeAlias   string         `json:"typeAlias,omitempty"`
    28→			Name        string         `json:"name"`
    29→			Heading     string         `json:"heading"`
    30→			Description string         `json:"description"`
    31→			Info        string         `json:"info"`
    32→			Options     []schema.Field `json:"options"`
    33→		}
    34→
    35→		result := make([]*NotifierPlugin, 0, len(v2))
    36→		for _, s := range v2 {
    37→			v1, ok := s.GetVersion(schema.V1)
    38→			if !ok {
    39→				continue
    40→			}
    41→			result = append(result, &NotifierPlugin{
    42→				Type:        string(s.Type),
    43→				Name:        s.Name,
    44→				Description: s.Description,
    45→				Heading:     s.Heading,
    46→				Info:        s.Info,
    47→				Options:     v1.Options,
    48→			})
    49→		}
    50→		return response.JSON(http.Sta

    39→	}

    42→	if err != nil {
    43→		return nil, err
    44→	}
    45→	postable.Settings = jsonBytes
    46→	return postable, nil

## Summary: Legacy Alerting Engine and Dashboard Alerts in Grafana Codebase

Based on my search of the Grafana codebase, I've identified the key files and architecture for the legacy alerting engine that was replaced by the unified alerting (ngalert) system. Here's what I found:

### 1. **Legacy Alert Database Schema** (Old Dashboard Alert Models)
**Location:** `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go`

This migration file defines the original dashboard alert system:
- **alert table** - Stores dashboard-level alerts with columns:
  - dashboard_id, panel_id (link to dashboard/panel)
  - name, message, state, settings
  - frequency, handler, severity
  - silenced, execution_error
  - eval_data, eval_date
  - new_state_date, state_changes
  - created, updated

- **alert_notification table** - Stores notification channels (legacy notifiers)
  - id, org_id, name, type, settings
  - is_default, frequency, send_reminder
  - disable_resolve_message, uid
  - secure_settings

- **alert_notification_state table** - Tracks notification delivery state
  - org_id, alert_id, notifier_id
  - state, version, updated_at
  - alert_rule_state_updated_version

- **alert_rule_tag table** - Tags for legacy alerts

### 2. **Unified Alerting (ngalert) System** - The Modern Replacement
**Location:** `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/services/ngalert/`

This is the new system that replaced the legacy engine with these main components:

#### Core Models:
- **AlertRule** (`/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go`)
  - NoDataState and ExecutionErrorState enums
  - Alert rule definitions with conditions, query templates, notification settings

- **AlertInstanc

    26→	}))

    23→func getDashboardFromEvent(event resource.WriteEvent) (*dashboard.Dashboard, error) {
    24→	obj, ok := event.Object.GetRuntimeObject()
    25→	if ok && obj != nil {
    26→		dash, ok := obj.(*dashboard.Dashboard)
    27→		if ok {
    28→			return dash, nil
    29→		}
    30→	}
    31→	dash := &dashboard.Dashboard{}
    32→	err := json.Unmarshal(event.Value, dash)
    33→	return dash, err
    34→}

    17→// 2. Always add new migrations (to change or undo previous migrations)
    18→// 3. Some migrations are not yet written (rename column, table, drop table, index etc)

    20→//    migrations may not be caught by integration tests unless feature flags are

    27→func (s *Service) getAlertMuteTimings(ctx context.Context, signedInUser *user.SignedInUser) ([]muteTimeInterval, error) {

    38→			MuteTimeInterval: config.MuteTimeInterval{
    39→				Name:          muteTiming.Name,
    40→				TimeIntervals: muteTiming.TimeIntervals,
    41→			},
    42→		})
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	return muteTimeIntervals, nil
    46→}
